Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper (arXiv:1108.0408)\n- `README.md` — description and error analysis\n- `proof/lean/KardashProof.lean` + `proof/rocq/KardashProof.v` — formalizing the claimed algorithm with `sorry`/`Admitted` at Theorem 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary If you have any issues with formalization, just make sure these issues are properly and fully documented in the code comments.\n\nAlso ensure the attempt folder have structure:\n\n- original/ (description of proof idea/text, and original proof text in pdf/html and conversion to of that text to markdown in all cases, markdown should be translated to English if original text is not in English, so we should have README.md, ORIGINAL.md (conversion result) and ORIGINAL.(pdf/html/...))\n- proof/ (the forward proof attempt, it should follow exactly the text of proof in markdown, showing each original line or paragraph, after that convert it to actual Lean and Rocq statements, actual Lean and Rocq files must be present in that folder, commenting all statements that will not compile, keeping compiled statements).\n- refutation/ (the proof against the original idea, should have refutations of refutable original statements from human proof)\n\nSo end result will be that will collect as much formalization as we can for each prompt attempt, so we later can reuse it in our research.\n\nUse https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/504 as example for file structure.\n\nMake sure scripts/check_attempt_structure.py script will put all ATTEMPTS.md in alphabetical order, to reduce probability of conflicts in the future.\nAlso execute scripts/check_attempt_structure.py to update ATTEMPTS.md after you finish.\n\nEnsure all changes are correct, consistent and fully meet the requirements.","author_association":"OWNER","pin":null,"reactions":{"url":"https://api.github.com/repos/konard/p-vs-np/issues/comments/4306025671/reactions","total_count":0,"+1":0,"-1":0,"laugh":0,"hooray":0,"confused":0,"heart":0,"rocket":0,"eyes":0},"performed_via_github_app":null}]

Here's a summary of what was done:\n\n## Summary\n\nCreated a full formalization for Sergey Kardash's 2011 P=NP attempt (Woeginger's list #76) at `proofs/attempts/sergey-kardash-2011-peqnp/`.\n\n**The attempt**: Kardash's \"pair cleaning\" method iteratively removes inconsistent variable assignments from overlapping clause groups in a k-CNF formula, claiming the result is non-empty iff satisfiable — giving O(n^12) for 3-SAT.\n\n**The error**: Pair cleaning is equivalent to **arc consistency (AC-3)** from constraint programming. Arc consistency is polynomial and necessary for satisfiability, but is **not sufficient** for k ≥ 3 — arc-consistent formulas can still be unsatisfiable. The fatal gap is in Lemma 1's inductive step, which unjustifiably treats local pairwise consistency as global satisfiability.\n\n**Files created**:\n- `ORIGINAL.md` + `ORIGINAL.pdf` — full paper (arXiv:1108.0408)\n- `README.md` — description and error analysis\n- `proof/lean/KardashProof.lean` + `proof/rocq/KardashProof.v` — formalizing the claimed algorithm with `sorry`/`Admitted` at Theorem 1\n- `refutation/lean/KardashRefutation.lean` + `refutation/rocq/KardashRefutation.v` — showing arc consistency ≠ satisfiability\n\nPR: https://github.com/konard/p-vs-np/pull/548\n\n---\n*This summary
